    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

  <span id="freeText1617143424628019141" style="display:none">A chance encounter in the dark leads eighteen-year-old Daniel and the girl who stumbles across him to profess their love for each other. But this love has conditions: they agree it will last only one hour, and it will be only make-believe.<br /><br />When their hour is up and the girl rushes off like Cinderella, Daniel tries to convince himself that what happened between them seemed perfect only because they were pretending it was. Moments like that happen only in fairy tales.<br /><br />One year and one bad relationship later, his disbelief in love-at-first-sight is stripped away the day he meets Six: a girl with a strange name and an even stranger personality. Unfortunately for Daniel, finding true love doesn"t guarantee a happily ever after... it only further threatens it.<br /><br />Will an unbearable secret from the past jeopardize Daniel and Six's only chance at saving each other?</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/730174745" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730174745?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730174745" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9759668710870727113"><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380438090ra/885528.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> I can’t stop smiling!! </b><br/><br/>Finding Cinderella was a beautifully written, deeply heart warming novella that made me laugh, cry, and fall in love. In less than 100 pages, it made me <i>feel</i> more than I have in many entire books. Daniel and Six captured my heart and I hope that one day we get more of their story because I’m not ready to let go yet!<br/><br/>I was originally going to talk about the plot here but honestly, I think it’ll be more fun to just discover it for yourselves. Suffice it to say that I absolut</span>
  <span id="freeText9759668710870727113" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380438090ra/885528.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> I can’t stop smiling!! </b><br><br>Finding Cinderella was a beautifully written, deeply heart warming novella that made me laugh, cry, and fall in love. In less than 100 pages, it made me <i>feel</i> more than I have in many entire books. Daniel and Six captured my heart and I hope that one day we get more of their story because I’m not ready to let go yet!<br><br>I was originally going to talk about the plot here but honestly, I think it’ll be more fun to just discover it for yourselves. Suffice it to say that I absolutely adored every word of story – it was fun, quirky and unique.<br><br>In case you don’t remember, Daniel and Six were Holder and Sky’s best friends from <i>Hopeless</i> and <i>Losing Hope</i> and while this novella reads as a standalone, it would have greater meaning if you read both those books first. Also, fans of Holder and Sky will be happy to know that they have several scenes in this and it was a real treat to see them from the outside through someone else’s eyes.<br><br>The character dynamics are just gold, the writing is witty and, true to Colleen Hoover’s style, you are made to care deeply about every part of these characters’ lives. I have quotes highlighted on each page and while the majority of the story kept me laughing out loud, swooning and chuckling to myself, there were also strong emotional reveals that had me in tears and brought a really wonderful depth to it all.<br><br>It was short enough to read in one sitting but long enough to never feel rushed and give you that feeling of reading a ‘complete’ story. I finished it with a huge smile on my face and the happiest feeling in my heart.<br><br>Truly, the perfect novella ♥<br><br>5 stars!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> It feels sort of euphoric, like we’re in some sort of fairy tale. Like she’s Tinkerbell and I’m Peter Pan. <br><br>No, wait. I don’t want to be Peter Pan.<br><br>Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><i> Quotes in this review are still subject to change before publication. A huge thank you to Colleen Hoover for sending me an early review copy!! </i><br><br>*******************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_730789182" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/730789182" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730789182?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730789182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17759792015305323773"><b>5 Cinderella Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/24dd135a-63d6-42d1-9cd2-a5eddea61fcc_zps08ac0d46.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381938954i/5447398.jpg' alt=' photo 24dd135a-63d6-42d1-9cd2-a5eddea61fcc_zps08ac0d46.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Colleen Hoover has done it again. I swear, this woman could not write a bad story if she tried. <i>Finding Cinderella</i>, as short as it was, is a new favorite of mine. <br/><br/>We meet Daniel (Holder’s best friend) and Six (Sky’s best friend) in <i>Hopeless</i>. Six and Daniel meet in a closet, although it’s dark and they don’t know one another, they connect. <br/><b>
  <blockquote>It feels sort of euphoric, like we’re in some sort of fairy tale. Like she’s Tinkerbell and I’m Peter Pan. <br/>No, wait. I don’t want t</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17759792015305323773" style="display:none"><b>5 Cinderella Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/24dd135a-63d6-42d1-9cd2-a5eddea61fcc_zps08ac0d46.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381938954i/5447398.jpg" alt=" photo 24dd135a-63d6-42d1-9cd2-a5eddea61fcc_zps08ac0d46.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Colleen Hoover has done it again. I swear, this woman could not write a bad story if she tried. <i>Finding Cinderella</i>, as short as it was, is a new favorite of mine. <br><br>We meet Daniel (Holder’s best friend) and Six (Sky’s best friend) in <i>Hopeless</i>. Six and Daniel meet in a closet, although it’s dark and they don’t know one another, they connect. <br><b>
  <blockquote>It feels sort of euphoric, like we’re in some sort of fairy tale. Like she’s Tinkerbell and I’m Peter Pan. <br>No, wait. I don’t want to be Peter Pan.<br>Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming.</blockquote>
</b> The time they spend together is over too soon. Daniel spends weeks looking for his Cinderella. Six goes off to Italy. They meet again about a year later, and hit it off. Neither one of them know that the person they are spending so much time with is the same person from the closet. The more time the two spend together, the more they start to feel for one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/c64a6fb5-fbc7-45e3-99b1-0a354c0f59fd_zps53de2cf5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381938954i/5447399.jpg" alt=" photo c64a6fb5-fbc7-45e3-99b1-0a354c0f59fd_zps53de2cf5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really fell for Daniel in <i>Losing Hope</i>. I was so excited to hear he was getting his own novella, with Six nonetheless. Daniel is the most lovable and hilarious character. One of the best parts about this novella is it’s from his point of view. I loved Daniel and Holder together... I know thats a random thing to say, but their little banters had me smiling so wide!<br> <blockquote>
  <i> “Daniel?” <br>“Holder?” <br>“What are you up to?”<br> “I do not know what you are talking about.” <br>“You do know what I am talking about because when you are lying, you do not use contractions when you speak.”<br><br>“For real,” I say. “You’re my best friend and I love you. I’m not ashamed to admit that I love a guy. I love you, Holder. Daniel Wesley loves Dean Holder. Always and forever.”<br>“Daniel, go make out with your girlfriend.”<br> “Not until you tell me you love me, too.”<br> “I fucking love you, now GO AWAY.” <br>I grin “I love you more.”</i>
</blockquote><br> This story was as close to perfection as they come. It was beautiful, heart warming, funny, and kept a smile on my face. Colleen Hoover’s writing is magical. It’s flawless. The only negative I have is the length- I wanted a whole Daniel book! I also want to say, I think it is AMAZING that this author gave her fans this novella for free. I would have gladly paid for it. Fan’s of Ms. Hoover’s works should pick this up. If you haven’t read <i>Hopeless</i> or <i>Losing Hope</i>, I would highly recommend reading them. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/698e5165-f21c-4ab8-9b59-b7f9bd59a816_zps8087c585.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381938954i/5447400.jpg" alt=" photo 698e5165-f21c-4ab8-9b59-b7f9bd59a816_zps8087c585.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17759792015305323773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_731022447" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/731022447" />
    <a title="K" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16359109-k"><img alt="K" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357989852p2/16359109.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/731022447?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/16359109-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=foul-mouthed-hero">foul-mouthed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=love-the-hero">love-the-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=hilarious">hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=heart-wrenching">heart-wrenching</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=love-the-heroine">love-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer731022447" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12872465211262909710"><b> 5 MOTHERF***KING ANGEL STARS!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381951321i/5464777._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I'll be her Prince Charming." ~Daniel </i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Once upon a time, there was a tiny maintenance closet; crowded, abandoned, a place to sleep or skip class. Here, in this small closet, Prince Charming met Cinderella.<br/><br/>Although originally all Prince Charming wanted was a place to avoid class or a place to take a quick nap, he encounters a woman who happens upon the closet he's in. They form an immediate connection, and fearing that on</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12872465211262909710" style="display:none"><b> 5 MOTHERF***KING ANGEL STARS!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381951321i/5464777._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I'll be her Prince Charming." ~Daniel </i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Once upon a time, there was a tiny maintenance closet; crowded, abandoned, a place to sleep or skip class. Here, in this small closet, Prince Charming met Cinderella.<br><br>Although originally all Prince Charming wanted was a place to avoid class or a place to take a quick nap, he encounters a woman who happens upon the closet he's in. They form an immediate connection, and fearing that once they turn the lights on they'll lose this perfect encounter,they decide to leave the lights off and pretend to be in love until the hour is up. That way they can have this perfect memory of one time in their lives where they at least pretended to love somebody.<br><br>When the clock strikes an hour, and their time is up, Cinderella flees. Never to be seen by Prince Charming again..."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't think there is a single thing about this story that I didn't love. Even though it was only a novella, it was <b>sweet, sexy, romantic, surprising, heart-wrenching, and breathtaking</b> all at the same time. I couldn't put this book down, and found myself having to carry my Kindle around the grocery store so that I could continue to read. I loved all the characters. They could make me cry in one instant and then the next second I would literally be laughing out loud. Colleen Hoover is one of the most talented authors I have ever had the honor of reading. <i>Finding Cinderella</i> is by far <u>the best novella I have ever read!</u><br><br><i>Finding Cinderella</i> is the story of a girl named <b>Six</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381954384i/5468515.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We all have deal breakers, Daniel. Some of us just hope we can keep them hidden forever." ~Six</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>She's the girl whose <b>name isn't even Six,</b> but she changed it because she was mad at parents when she was 14 and has refused to be called anything else since.<br> <br>She's the girl who <b>doesn't carry purses</b>, for all she needs is the keys in her pocket. <br><br>She's the girl who <b>likes the wind in her hair, fist bumps, and the merry go round. </b><br><br>She's also unfortunately the girl with a <b>reputation for being a slut</b> who's slept with way too many guys, and yet has never even held a guys hand before or gone on a date. <i>that's her sad truth...</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I love how much you love me." ~Six</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Then Cinderella meets Prince Charming, I mean <b>Daniel</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381956996i/5473824._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Because we show up, Six. It's what we do. It's me and you, babe." ~Daniel</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Daniel is best friends with Holder and when spending time with Holder and Holder's girlfriend Sky, he meets Six. We were introduced to Holder and Sky in the previous installment <i>Hopeless</i>. I'm glad we got glimpses of Holder and Sky again. I had missed them. They were handled perfectly in Finding Cinderella. We find out a bit more of what happens with them, yet they don't overpower the story. When Daniel and Sky meet, Sky has a spoon in her mouth eating ice cream, and it's literally spoon at first sight. It's <b>intense, fast paced, and is making both of them have doubts wondering if things are just too good to be true.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It feels like her air just became my air and I suddenly want to take in fewer breaths in order to ensure she never runs out." ~Daniel</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved reading them fall in love. They had such an intense connection from the beginning and it was a true joy to read. There is even some surprises along the way that will completely shock you. I'm going to avoid saying too much on that subject for I don't want to spoil anything for anyone. JUST GO PICK THIS UP RIGHT NOW IT'S FREE!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381956464ra/5473013.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"That's exactly what this feels like. Like she's a drug I've become immediately addicted to but I have none in supply."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381957676ra/5474433.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She wants this to work with me as much as I want it to work with her and seeing the look in her eyes right now makes me believe that it will. I've never believed in anything like I believe in us." ~Daniel </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I will <i>always</i> wish for more where Colleen Hoover is concerned. I would be lying if I said that I felt this was enough of Daniel and Six. I don't. I feel like their story should continue. I feel like they have infinite possibilities, but if Colleen Hoover does end their story here, and we never hear any more from Daniel and Six, I know in my heart that they'll get their HEA one day. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381958724i/5475282._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12872465211262909710" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer743201841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4214674506778180821"><br/><br/><b>
  <i>WHAT I THOUGHT I WAS GETTING</i>
</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385110262i/7068975._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>WHAT I ACTUALLY GOT</i>
</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385110262ra/7068976.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>Despite the fact I don't normally read YA/NA, I wanted to try this novella since all my friends love it, I've not read Colleen Hoover and I have two teenage nieces to whom I was hoping to recommend this book and author. <br/><br/>This author does have a lovely writing style. But my problems with this started in the prologue and I simply couldn't get past them, even though there were parts of this I enjoyed.<br/><br/>When the title and blurb uses the words <b>
</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4214674506778180821" style="display:none"><br><br><b>
  <i>WHAT I THOUGHT I WAS GETTING</i>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385110262i/7068975._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b>
  <i>WHAT I ACTUALLY GOT</i>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385110262ra/7068976.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Despite the fact I don't normally read YA/NA, I wanted to try this novella since all my friends love it, I've not read Colleen Hoover and I have two teenage nieces to whom I was hoping to recommend this book and author. <br><br>This author does have a lovely writing style. But my problems with this started in the prologue and I simply couldn't get past them, even though there were parts of this I enjoyed.<br><br>When the title and blurb uses the words <b>
  <i>Cinderella</i>
</b> and <b>
  <i>fairytales</i>
</b> to describe this book....and the main characters are <b>
  <i>17/18</i>
</b> years of age....and the author’s profile states she writes <b>
  <i>young adult,</i>
</b> I’m expecting something along these lines....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382221943i/5758670._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br>....you know, a <i>slowly-building</i> story of sweet, first love that the protagonists find as teenagers and that lasts a lifetime. <br><br>When the blurb says...<i>a chance encounter in the dark</i>....<b>
  <i>this</i>
</b> is what I'm expecting....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382221943i/5758671.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Instead</i>....<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Of this...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382224718ra/5759880.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I got this...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382224673ra/5759857.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Two <b><i>teenagers,</i></b> two <b><i>strangers,</i></b> who have sex on their <b><i>second meeting</i></b> at <b><i>school</i></b> in the <b><i>janitor's closet</i></b> during <b><i>school hours.</i></b> <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382222342ra/5758896.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>These kids' sex education must have come straight from Chef.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738525.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738526.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738527.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738528.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Except that Daniel sounds like eighteen going on thirty-eight when he tells Six he's going to <b><i>make love</i></b> to her for <b><i>forty-five minutes</i></b>....yeah, like an <b><i>eighteen year-old boy</i></b> is going to do that instead of <i>wham-bam-thank-you-mam</i>....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382228498ra/5761621.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Six <i>hated everybody,</i> though I'm not quite sure why....<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738530.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[....maybe it was just a teenage thing. Or maybe it was because she felt used and abused by the relationships she'd been in. Though that doesn't make sense as she never said she was forced, or the sex with her <b>six</b> different partners was anything but consensual. It just came across as self-hatred for being sexually active/promiscuous. This sort of double standard in romances tends to irk me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738524.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382181388ra/5738529.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Since I've not read many YA's, the heroines' names may be par-for-the-course for this genre. We find out that <i>Six</i> is just the nickname for the heroine. Okay. But her <i>real</i> name is....<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b><i>Seven.</i></b> I suppose we'll also find out her father is The Count. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382229989i/5762300.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The names just seemed <i>silly.</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Towards the end there was a big twist/secret/bombshell that almost got the big brush-off.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382229989ra/5762301.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Something this big and important should have been given a bit more time.<br><br>I know this is fiction, I know it's for young adults and I know there was nothing explicit, but this just didn't work for me. Guess I can cross Colleen Hoover off my Christmas list for the nieces this year. This one's going on my <i>everyone-loves-but-Jill</i> shelf.<br><br>Now for something completely different, read my lovely friend, Jen's 5-star <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734249702" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a>.<br><br><b>Steam:</b> 1.5<br><br><i>* Thanks for the recommendation, Jen!</i><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8721203753753346067"> <b>5 Heartwarming Stars!!</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381709943i/5212787.jpg' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>	<br/>Daniel (Holder’s best-friend, in the doubtfully case you’ve forgotten.) found a girl in a maintenance closet a year ago. They never saw each other’s faces, they never found out their names, but they fell in love inside a closet.<br/>Until one day she suddenly stops appearing in the closed and leaving him broken to never heard from her again until now, one year after. <br/>The girl is no one else but Six, who went to Italy through a student-change program (Yeah, you also remember h</span>
  <span id="freeText8721203753753346067" style="display:none"> <b>5 Heartwarming Stars!!</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381709943i/5212787.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">	<br>Daniel (Holder’s best-friend, in the doubtfully case you’ve forgotten.) found a girl in a maintenance closet a year ago. They never saw each other’s faces, they never found out their names, but they fell in love inside a closet.<br>Until one day she suddenly stops appearing in the closed and leaving him broken to never heard from her again until now, one year after. <br>The girl is no one else but Six, who went to Italy through a student-change program (Yeah, you also remember her. Sky’s best-friend.) And when a year after they meet again they fall in love again… without having the slightest idea that they already fell in love once. <br>But a year changes a lot of things and maybe the people who fell in love inside a dark closet, are not the same ones who fell in love in the open air. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381709943i/5212788.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I first read Losing Hope I remember thinking that I would love to read a book about Daniel’s story because he was pretty much awesome. He did not disappoint, far from it. <br>I also remember thinking that Six was pretty cool and a great friend. She did not disappoint as well. <br>Their story was extremely sweet and made me feel warm and giddy. Loved every single second of it. (Especially their sense of humor. I laughed real hard with those two!)<br>If you read the previous books (Sky and Dean’s story) you will LOVE this novella. If you haven’t… what the hell are you waiting for??! </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730286788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3601977681997947660"><b>SIX stars!!!!</b><br/><br/>I heart Colleen Hoover. Hard. I think the only thing that might make me love her more is if she wrote a book with sex in it. She can write a book boyfriend, a male lead, a hero like none other!!!! And Daniel was no exception!! <br/><br/>I LOVED Daniel.<br/>I LOVED Six.<br/>I LOVED how they met.<br/>I LOVED how they fell in love.<br/>I LOVED their banter. <br/>I LOVED Daniel's family--SO funny.<br/>I LOVED LOVED LOVED every.single.thing about this book!<br/><br/>Group hug!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476783284" href="/book/show/20733636-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=paperback">paperback</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1468893792" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1150442129475719818">Screw it, this book made me smile the entire time so it gets <b> 5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “I don't even know if people should use the working fucking and angel in the same thought structure, but shit. She really looks like a fucking angel..” </i> </b><br/><br/>There's something about Colleen Hoover novellas, I tend to love them more than her full length novels. Which is so rare because most of the time novellas don't have enough. But this book in its entirety and shortness made me fall in love with it. <br/><br/><b> Finding Cinderella </b> is abo</span>
  <span id="freeText1150442129475719818" style="display:none">Screw it, this book made me smile the entire time so it gets <b> 5 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “I don't even know if people should use the working fucking and angel in the same thought structure, but shit. She really looks like a fucking angel..” </i> </b><br><br>There's something about Colleen Hoover novellas, I tend to love them more than her full length novels. Which is so rare because most of the time novellas don't have enough. But this book in its entirety and shortness made me fall in love with it. <br><br><b> Finding Cinderella </b> is about Holder's best friend Daniel. After a chance encounter in a closet in school, Daniel met and lost his dream girl without ever seeing her face. A year later, and a failed drama filled relationship later, Daniel is introduced to Sky's friend Six who has returned from Italy after a year abroad. The two have an instant chemistry and begin dating, but both have secrets than can be deal breakers for the other. <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421135336i/13327545.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> <i> “I can't take you tonight. I had my heart completely broken about an hour ago by a psychotic bitch and I need a little more time to recover from that relationship. How about tomorrow night?” </i> </b><br><br>I'm glad I read this right after reading Losing Hope, that book is definitely meant to be read before reading this one. Yes this book is a standalone, but you gain a lot more by reading the other two books first. I loved reading Six and Daniel's book, I had a gigantic smile on my face the entire time. I loved both characters and their unconventional romance.<br><br>Leave it to Colleen Hoover to write a funny book and one packed with all the feels at the same time. I found myself rooting for this couple from the very beginning and would love to see more of them in the future. If you need something light and something that will make you happy, this is the book for you.<br><br><b> <i> “It blows my mind that I get to love you.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/RRR.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444273756i/16478167._SX540_.png" alt=" photo RRR.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <span id="freeText14136329226153530641" style="display:none"><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Thank you Colleen Hoover for gifting this book to the reading world! I wish I had your flare with words to perfectly express how much I truly adore your books. Each one of your characters holds a special place in my heart. Now, Daniel and Six have a spot as well. <div id="review_730933487" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/730933487" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730933487?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730933487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16740431115193049322"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’ve never believed in anything like I believe in the possibility of the two of us.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Oh my God, can this woman write a bad book just for kicks? No, this is not just a novella, it is not just a little add-on story to an already stellar series, and this is definitely not a re-hash of anything we’ve already seen in <i>Hopeless</i> or <i>Losing Hope</i> – this is the story that fills all the little gaps we never even knew needed filling and it is the story that makes us fall in love with the two secon</span>
  <span id="freeText16740431115193049322" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’ve never believed in anything like I believe in the possibility of the two of us.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Oh my God, can this woman write a bad book just for kicks? No, this is not just a novella, it is not just a little add-on story to an already stellar series, and this is definitely not a re-hash of anything we’ve already seen in <i>Hopeless</i> or <i>Losing Hope</i> – this is the story that fills all the little gaps we never even knew needed filling and it is the story that makes us fall in love with the two secondary characters as much as we loved Holder and Sky. It is also a testament to the fact that Colleen Hoover doesn’t need 400 pages to make you feel with every crevice of your heart and that when it comes to telling a story through witty but emotionally-charged dialogues or creating loveable, engaging characters, she is unrivalled. I knew this story would be great but I never even imagined a novella could be this spectacular.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I don’t even know your phone number,” I say.<br>“I don’t even know your birthday,” she says.<br>“You’re the worst girlfriend I’ve ever had.”</i>
</blockquote><br>We met Daniel and Six in previous instalments of the series as Holder and Sky’s best friends, two outspoken, sarcastic, but fiercely loyal individuals who supported their best friends through thick and thin, and now we get to see them in the limelight. By knowing all the other characters and the main storyline in such detail, no time is wasted on introductions or setups of scenes – we get to immediately zoom into their story and enjoy the ride.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“How do you make love to someone you aren’t in love with?”<br>I lean forward until my mouth is next to her ear. “We pretend.”</i>
</blockquote><br>I refuse to spoil any of their story for you, however, not because of its length, but because I knew very little going in and I am grateful for that as not knowing what to expect was half the fun in this case. I will only tell you that their tale starts with one fated encounter that forever changes who they are and what they hope to find in life. The rest of their story is a delightful account of a boy and a girl falling head over heels for one another, and learning what love is through that experience. Their captivating personalities and the amusing dialogues between them drive the story forward and keep us engrossed page after page.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Are you a witch? … I have no idea who you even are and now you’re my damn girlfriend. What the hell have you done to me?”</i>
</blockquote><br>This is a book that had me laughing out loud, constantly catching myself smiling like a fool, and even had me shed a few heart-clenching tears at times. My emotions were all over the place because every word meant something, every scene counted, and every sentence struck the right chord. If you’ve loved <i>Hopeless</i> and <i>Losing Hope</i> as desperately as I have, I have no doubt that you will adore Six and Daniel’s beautiful story. They say you can’t improve on perfection – I guess Ms Hoover just did.<br><br><i>While this story could be read as a standalone novella, I personally would not recommend doing so without first reading the other two books in the series as it follows a parallel timeline and some knowledge of events and other characters would enhance the overall reading experience.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Stop! Stop saying things that make me grin like an idiot. My face has been hurting since the second I met you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2013/10/06/finding-cinderella-colleen-hoover/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16740431115193049322" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_730780343" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/730780343" />
    <a title="Miriam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10072078-miriam"><img alt="Miriam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383915365p2/10072078.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730780343?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miriam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miriam" href="/user/show/10072078-miriam">Miriam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">all Colleen Hoover fangirls</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Miriam by: </span>
      My fangirling self
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=5-golden-stars">5-golden-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=short-stories">short-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=heartwrenchingly-angsty">heartwrenchingly-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=favourite-book-boyfriends">favourite-book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730780343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3652426624909636388"><b>
  <blockquote>“Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><b>Let's face it</b>. I knew this was going to be amazing. It's practically Colleen Hoover's trademark to work magic with literature and <i>Finding Cinderella</i> was no exception.<br/><br/>But I didn't know that it was going to be <i>this</i> amazing. I didn't know it was going to be the type of amazing that would just blow me away without failure. And all in a hundred pages. That's the thing. All in a hundred-and-five pages. That's short. And to make me </span>
  <span id="freeText3652426624909636388" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>Let's face it</b>. I knew this was going to be amazing. It's practically Colleen Hoover's trademark to work magic with literature and <i>Finding Cinderella</i> was no exception.<br><br>But I didn't know that it was going to be <i>this</i> amazing. I didn't know it was going to be the type of amazing that would just blow me away without failure. And all in a hundred pages. That's the thing. All in a hundred-and-five pages. That's short. And to make me fall in love with Daniel and Six that quickly? That's nothing short of miraculous.<br><br><b>
  <u>My Daniel Wesley and Seven Marie Six Cinderella Jacobs</u>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382259662i/5775778.jpg" width="230" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Daniel and Six were the couple that I never thought would feel right together, but once I actually thought about it, I could never actually see what was wrong with them being together in the first place. They're the most unlikely, yet perfect couple and I just love them together. I love how Daniel just throws every fibre of his body into his and Six's relationship and isn't afraid of how quickly he's falling in love.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>That’s exactly what this feels like. Like she’s a drug I’ve become immediately addicted to but I have none in supply. The only thing that satiates the craving is her laugh. Or her smile or her kiss or the feel of her pressed against me.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The romance between them <i>feels</i> natural. I guess some people can label it as insta-love/love-at-first-sight (something I despise with my entire being), but it doesn't feel like that to me. It feels like two people who, from the first moment they met, <i>understood</i> each other on a deeper level. They <i>connected</i>.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “It’s different with Six, though. Not only does she get my sense of humor and my personality, but I feel like she encourages it. I feel like the real me is what she likes the most and every time she laughs or smiles at the perfect moment, I want to fist bump her.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>They didn't fall in love at first sight but the most pivotal moment in the story was when Cinderella fell into Prince Charming's closet and they decided to comfort each other.<br><br>They spun their own fairytale. And in that fairytale, Daniel found his Cinderella.<br><br>So before I read <i>Finding Cinderella</i>, I compiled a list of things I wanted to happen which you can see below.<br><br><b><i><u>Thing I Wanted To Happen:</u></i><br><br>- Sky/Hope and Holder scenes?<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382258965i/5775359._SY540_.jpg" width="20" height="20" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>- BRECKIN scenes?<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382258965i/5775359._SY540_.jpg" width="20" height="20" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>- Six and Daniel's HEA?<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382258965i/5775359._SY540_.jpg" width="20" height="20" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>-Since it's cool to refer to oneself in third person, Miriam's mind blown? <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382258965i/5775359._SY540_.jpg" width="20" height="20" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </b><br><br>So as you can see, my every single demand ended up being satisfied. <br><br><b>But here's the thing.</b><br><br>I might be satisfied <i>(which I am)</i> but that doesn't mean I <i>don't</i> want more <i>(Which I do. I really, really do.)</i> The few peeks I got of Sky and Dean and reading from Daniel's perspective is just making me hungry for more. Longing for more.<br><br>It's like this gaping hole in my stomach and that's all I can describe it as. It might actually be life-threatening! (Well, it's not but who says I don't have a taste for the theatrics)<br><br>And to end this review (if it even is a review because mostly it's just me gushing or praying for another short story), I'm just going to use a couple of song lyrics from The Avett Brothers (which coincidentally is a band that was introduced to me in <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Slammed</a>
</i> as well as slam poetry and now I'm addicted to them. Anyway, if Daniel and Six's story was made into a movie, I just strongly felt that should be made into a soundtrack. <br><br><b>
  <i>"...Then you came back from space<br>With a brand new laugh and a different face<br>You took my hand and held it up<br>And shot my arm full of love.<br><br>"And it spread<br>And it spread into the world <br>And it spread<br>And it spread into the world."</i>
</b><br><br>-The Avett Brothers, <i>And It Spread</i><br><br>5++++++++++++++++++ stars<br><br><u>*Favourite Quotes</u><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“What’s your deal, then?”<br>“What do you mean?”<br>“Everyone has something and I can’t figure yours out. You know, that one thing about themselves that’s eventually a deal-breaker.” I crank the car and begin to back out. “I want to know what yours is right now. My heart can’t take another second of these tiny little things you do that drive me completely insane.”<br><br><br>"We stare at each other for so long I begin to worry that she’s put some kind of spell on me, because I’ve never wanted to just stare at a girl like I want to stare at her. Just looking at her causes my heart to burn and my chest to constrict."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>*Novella can be read as a stand-alone but if you haven't read<i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717943.Hopeless__Hopeless___1_" title="Hopeless (Hopeless, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Hopeless</a></i> or <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17340050.Losing_Hope__Hopeless___2_" title="Losing Hope (Hopeless, #2) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Losing Hope</a></i>, then clearly you're missing out.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3652426624909636388" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730557073" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12074281940111545641">A modern day Cinderella story but instead of a ballroom where Prince Charming meets Cinderella it is a high school maintenance closet. <br/><br/><b>Daniel</b> is Prince Charming and <b>Six</b> is Cinderella. These two were supporting characters from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717943.Hopeless__Hopeless___1_' title='Hopeless (Hopeless, #1) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Hopeless</a>. <i> Finding Cinderella </i> is from Daniel's POV. If you haven't read Hopeless it's okay because <i>Finding Cinderella</i> can be read as <b>standalone</b>.<br/><br/>Christmas has arrived early and Ms. Hoover gifted everyone this novella.Thank you, Ms. Hoover, for the amazing gift. Your story t</span>
  <span id="freeText12074281940111545641" style="display:none">A modern day Cinderella story but instead of a ballroom where Prince Charming meets Cinderella it is a high school maintenance closet. <br><br><b>Daniel</b> is Prince Charming and <b>Six</b> is Cinderella. These two were supporting characters from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717943.Hopeless__Hopeless___1_" title="Hopeless (Hopeless, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Hopeless</a>. <i> Finding Cinderella </i> is from Daniel's POV. If you haven't read Hopeless it's okay because <i>Finding Cinderella</i> can be read as <b>standalone</b>.<br><br>Christmas has arrived early and Ms. Hoover gifted everyone this novella.Thank you, Ms. Hoover, for the amazing gift. Your story telling skills never ceases to amaze me. <br><br>*Pre-review* <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>**PRE-ORDER this free novella**</b><br><br><b>**FREE**</b> novella by Ms. Hoover coming out on October 14th.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380735154ra/3116681.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717943.Hopeless__Hopeless___1_" title="Hopeless (Hopeless, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_731063827" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/731063827" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/731063827?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer731063827" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7078624554856087271"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Don't open your eyes... Give me ten more seconds to stare, because you look absolutely beautiful right now</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Finding Cinderella is an adorable read and any Colleen Hoover fan will be jumping for joy and wishing for more</b><br/><br/><b>5 Adorable Stars</b><br/><br/>Honestly, I don't think I was in the best frame of mind in reading this, so my review may be a little off base. Yes, I'm a major Colleen Hoover fan, yes I've read all of her books, but I guess when it comes down to it, I'm just not a fan of novellas.<br/><br/>This i</span>
  <span id="freeText7078624554856087271" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Don't open your eyes... Give me ten more seconds to stare, because you look absolutely beautiful right now</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>Finding Cinderella is an adorable read and any Colleen Hoover fan will be jumping for joy and wishing for more</b><br /><br /><b>5 Adorable Stars</b><br /><br />Honestly, I don't think I was in the best frame of mind in reading this, so my review may be a little off base. Yes, I'm a major Colleen Hoover fan, yes I've read all of her books, but I guess when it comes down to it, I'm just not a fan of novellas.<br /><br />This is Daniel and Six's story. Daniel is Holder's best friend and Six is Sky's best friend. Daniel and Six meet in a closet and forge an instant connection, brief, but strong. One year later, both meet up again, but not knowing who each other really are.<br /><br />I love the beginning, I thought it was very cute (yes a bit cheesy at times), but that's the stuff we love right? Colleen really has a way with words and for obvious reasons that is why she is so loved.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I don't even really want to make out with you because I like talking to you too much<br /><br />Put your hands on my face and push me against this wall and slip me some tongue! Now!</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>I LOVED the banter between Daniel and Six.</b> I did laugh out loud at a lot of parts and yes I thought to myself, damn Colleen can write some whitty shit. It amazes me.<br /><br />I have a personal problem, so when ever it resurfaces in books, it makes me cringe. So, yes I did cringe and I kind was like, oh boy it went there. I think it would have been easier on me if it wasn't a novella and I got more character development or I was more wrapped in the story, but I can't fault anyone for that, b/c it's novella. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>We all have deal-breakers, Daniel. Some of us just hope we can keep them hidden forever</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />So, yes, Finding Cinderella is an adorable read, it's a Colleen read and YAY for releasing it as <b>FREE</b> we fans love you for it.<br /><br />And like many readers, I'm gonna say this... <b>GIVE ME MORE!</b><br /><br />For more reviews, visit <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7078624554856087271" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

And unfortunately, the whole story wasn't that believable. At least not to me. I didn't like Six in Hopeless, so I didn't expect to like her here either. She's, however, an okay character. I liked Daniel a bit better but he's not a perfect character in any way. And, of course, Colleen had to go and stab my heart at the very end.   <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=tissues-required">tissues-required</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=freebie">freebie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734249702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7012894479380555126"><b>
  <i>I laugh and clutch at my heart. "Dammit, Six. I love every single word that comes out of your mouth."<br/>"Cock," she says dryly. She's evil.<br/>"Except that word," I say. "I don't love cock."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Can someone find a way for me to rate this higher than 5 stars? 'Cause yeah, that's what needs to happen right about now. This little novella (little novella, people!) managed to wring more emotion out of me than most full length books. <br/><br/>Six and Daniel are delightful together. The fact that I used the word "delig</span>
  <span id="freeText7012894479380555126" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>I laugh and clutch at my heart. "Dammit, Six. I love every single word that comes out of your mouth."<br />"Cock," she says dryly. She's evil.<br />"Except that word," I say. "I don't love cock."</i>
</b><br /><br />Can someone find a way for me to rate this higher than 5 stars? 'Cause yeah, that's what needs to happen right about now. This little novella (little novella, people!) managed to wring more emotion out of me than most full length books. <br /><br />Six and Daniel are delightful together. The fact that I used the word "delightful" in a review should tell you just how much I loved this story! There's no other word for it, though. Every conversation, even the eventual angsty ones, were so natural and entertaining in a way that made me actually want to meet these characters. I'll admit to feeling a little creepy about having book crushes on both Daniel and Six but I've moved on from that. Now I'm just thinking about the fact that I'm jealous of all the folks that get to read this one for the first time.<br /><br /><b>Well done in a big way, Colleen Hoover. Well Done!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7012894479380555126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <a title="Kelly (and the Book Boar)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly (and the Book Boar)" href="/user/show/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar">Kelly (and the Book Boar)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1099931342" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14280003086843075481">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415389108ra/11781797.gif' alt='Commercial Photography' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>You might be asking yourself, “why would a shriveled up old hag like <b>
  <i>her</i>
</b> be reading <i>Finding Cinderella</i>????” The answer is quite simple:<br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415389108i/11781798._SY540_.jpg' alt='Commercial Photography' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Any author who has a memento copy of one of their books printed in “Ermahgerd” is someone who deserves to be read. Also, <i>Finding Cinderella</i> was free, so it was the obvious winner of the “which one should I read?” contest.<br/><br/>That being said, NA is soooooo not my bag. I <b>am</b> old and have a very low</span>
  <span id="freeText14280003086843075481" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415389108ra/11781797.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You might be asking yourself, “why would a shriveled up old hag like <b>
  <i>her</i>
</b> be reading <i>Finding Cinderella</i>????” The answer is quite simple:<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415389108i/11781798._SY540_.jpg" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Any author who has a memento copy of one of their books printed in “Ermahgerd” is someone who deserves to be read. Also, <i>Finding Cinderella</i> was free, so it was the obvious winner of the “which one should I read?” contest.<br><br>That being said, NA is soooooo not my bag. I <b>am</b> old and have a very low threshold when it comes to tolerating angst and I get a bit bitey when I read it . . . . <b>but</b> I totally understand the allure. If I were a young puppy again I would seriously <i>love</i> to be able to download freebies like this on the Kindle rather than being forced to steal my mom’s old Jackie Collins’ paperbacks in order to read something steamy. Now those things were horrible. *shudder*<br><br>I’m assuming if you <b>are</b> a fan of NA, <i>Finding Cinderella</i> is one that could receive a much higher rating along with a rave review, but please note a 3 Star rating from me is pretty dang solid. Even though I saw the big “a-ha” moment WAY before it ever came to light, it was still pretty much alright with me. Colleen Hoover writes a decent story with relatable characters who have great wit about them. I didn't have high expectations going in and was pleasantly surprised by how much I actually enjoyed myself. And while I assumed the main characters would <i>have</i> to experience "instalove" (if for no other reason than the fact that this was a novella), what I didn't expect was that <b>I</b> would end up kind of loving Daniel:<br><br><b>
  <i>“She fist bumped me. It’s not my fault. She hates purses and she fist bumped me, then she made me push her on the damn merry-go-round. After that, she demanded to see where I had sex in the park, then she forced me to sneak into my own bedroom. She’s weird and half the time I can’t keep up with her, but she thinks I’m funny as hell. And Chunk asked me this morning if I wanted to love her someday, and I realized I’ve never hoped I could love someone more than I want to love her.”</i>
</b><br><br>(a leading male who isn’t a super-assholey-bad-boy??? who’d a thunk it????)<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415389108ra/11781799.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yeah, yeah, I know: “Why don’t you have a seat over there” and all that jazz. I already registered myself on the sexual predator list, thank you very much Chris Hansen.<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415389108ra/11781800.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

<div id="review_733725545" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733725545" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/733725545?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733725545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12720140876297093661"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br/><br/>✮ First off, I'd really like to recommend that you read at least the first book in the series <i>before</i> you read this one. It's not necessary but I think you will have more of a feel of the story and what it's about. <br/><br/>✮ That being said...from reading the other books, I always felt like Daniel was a bit strange so I was pleasantly surprised! <br/><br/>✮ And I'm really glad we got more of Six. I feel like we got cheated out of her in the first book. <br/><br/>✮ I would definitely classify this as more NA </span>
  <span id="freeText12720140876297093661" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>✮ First off, I'd really like to recommend that you read at least the first book in the series <i>before</i> you read this one. It's not necessary but I think you will have more of a feel of the story and what it's about. <br><br>✮ That being said...from reading the other books, I always felt like Daniel was a bit strange so I was pleasantly surprised! <br><br>✮ And I'm really glad we got more of Six. I feel like we got cheated out of her in the first book. <br><br>✮ I would definitely classify this as more NA than YA. That closet scene was a bit intense. Heck, even their kisses are intense!<br><br>✮ Love Daniel with his nicknames and how it's finally explained!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383525861i/6586925.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✮ I enjoyed their sarcasm, teasing and being honest with each other.<br><br>✮ Of course, there was not enough Holder but I liked how he forbade Daniel to date Six. <br><br>✮ And Daniel's family with their reverse psychology! <br><br>✮ Bombshell...I was not expecting that! <br><br>✮ Please tell me there will be another book!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380297635ra/682340.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298441ra/683858.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>❀ “Don’t open your eyes,” I whisper, still staring at her. “Give me ten more seconds to stare, because you look absolutely beautiful right now.”<br><br>❀ “I don’t even know your phone number,” I say. <br><br>“I don’t even know your birthday,” she says. <br><br>“You’re the worst girlfriend I’ve ever had.”<br><br>❀ “For real,” I say. “You’re my best friend and I love you. I’m not ashamed to admit that I love a guy. I love you, Holder. Daniel Wesley loves Dean Holder. Always and forever.”<br><br>❀ "Daniel Wesley, where'd you learn those smooth moves?" <br><br>I laugh. "Not moves, Six. Charisma.” <br></span>

So thank you very much my Queen. :) I really loved and also lived this book. And people, believe me this book should be at least 1000 pages.   <span id="freeText7594990737879368411" style="display:none">First of all Colleen, I love you. You're my all time favorite author. I love your sense of humor and I really love when you describe feelings. So thank you very much my Queen. :) I really loved and also lived this book. And people, believe me this book should be at least 1000 pages. I just can't get enough of it. :) I laughed too much but in the end I cried. I cried like a baby. Colleen, you always did this to me. If you read Hopeless and Losing Hope books, you must read this book immediately. It was phenomenal and trust me, you'll be in love Daniel too as much as Holder. (^_^) <br><br>My God, I wanna write you whole book people but I shouldn't have to give you spoilers. So, go read it asap...   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s">books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer731204183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6002945254196311473">5 STARS, but really there aren't enough Stars to rate this book!!!!!<br/>Finding Cinderella was absolutely, positively, pure PERFECTION!!!<br/><br/>THANK YOU Colleen Hoover, for writing such an AMAZING story, AND for making it FREE!!<br/>That just shows just how incredible you truly are!<br/>This book was so flippin good!!!!!<br/><br/>This is the story of Daniel and Six, best friends to Holder and Sky, of course these two have to be amazing, to be their best friends!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps90036a81.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
