</a><br/><br/>I just LOVE Colleen Hoover's writing style.<br/>I found myself hi</span>
  <span id="freeText6002945254196311473" style="display:none">5 STARS, but really there aren't enough Stars to rate this book!!!!!<br>Finding Cinderella was absolutely, positively, pure PERFECTION!!!<br><br>THANK YOU Colleen Hoover, for writing such an AMAZING story, AND for making it FREE!!<br>That just shows just how incredible you truly are!<br>This book was so flippin good!!!!!<br><br>This is the story of Daniel and Six, best friends to Holder and Sky, of course these two have to be amazing, to be their best friends!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps90036a81.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381723189i/5234486._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps90036a81.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I just LOVE Colleen Hoover's writing style.<br>I found myself highlighting way too many excerpts from this book.<br>Daniel is just as amazing as ever, and so incredibly hysterical.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Nothing. They forgot to assign me a class, so I hide out in this maintenance closet every day for an hour."</b>
</i> - Daniel<br><br>He has quite an encounter with a mystery girl who stumbles into that closet he's been hiding out in.<br><br>A year later, Six is back from her study abroad program in Italy and she's starting school with the rest of the gang.<br>She and Daniel have an instant attraction to each other.<br>They try to keep their budding romance a secret.<br><br><br><b>Holy shit, she's cute. Her hair is lighter than I thought it was last night in Sky's room. Her skin is flawless. It's like she's the same girl from last night, only now she's in HD. And I was right. She really does look like a fucking angel.</b> - Daniel<br><br>Six is not the same girl she was before she went away a year ago.<br>She's turned a new leaf and there is something that haunts her.<br> <br>I loved how these two connected and let me just say that Daniel is just as swoon worthy as Holder!!<br><br><b>Whatever this is between us, neither one of us was searching for it. Neither one of us knew it even existed. Neither one of us is even remotely prepared for it, but I know we both want it. She wants this to work with me as much as I want it to work with her and seeing the look in her eyes right now makes me believe that it will. I've never believed in anything like I believe in the possibility of the two of us.</b> - Daniel<br><br>It was great to get more of Holder, Sky, and Breckin again.<br>Daniel's family is pretty amazing as well. They definitely brought a lot of humor to this story!!<br><br>There is a big reveal towards the end, that I DID NOT see coming and it is heart breaking.<br>Everyone should read this novella!!<br>If you're a fan of Colleen Hoover and you loved "Hopeless" and "Losing Hope", you definitely will LOVE this story!!<br><br>And here's one more excerpt from the book that solidified a place on my Top Book Boyfriends list for Daniel.<br><br><b>Her eyes focus on mine and she takes both my hands, then laces her fingers through them. We stare at each other like we've done so many times before, but this time I feel it in every single part of me. I feel</b> <i>
  <b>her</b>
</i> <b>in every part of me and the feeling is new and heavy and intense and I realize in this moment that we just became so much more together than we could ever possibly be alone.</b> - Daniel<br><br></span>

    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737337992?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737337992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2861601877886152854">We absolutely LOVED this book! We were going to do a traditional read and review for this one but decided against it. As this book was written and provided free to her readers as a "thank you" for their continued support,we wanted to give our followers who wouldn't normally write a review the opportunity to share their thoughts on Finding Cinderella and that post can be found on our blog here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/10/16/finding-cinderella-hopeless-series-2-5-by-colleen-hoover-some-of-our-fellow-readers-have-their-say/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/10/...</a><br/><br/>We did want to share this thought. We recently asked Colleen Ho</span>
  <span id="freeText2861601877886152854" style="display:none">We absolutely LOVED this book! We were going to do a traditional read and review for this one but decided against it. As this book was written and provided free to her readers as a "thank you" for their continued support,we wanted to give our followers who wouldn't normally write a review the opportunity to share their thoughts on Finding Cinderella and that post can be found on our blog here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/10/16/finding-cinderella-hopeless-series-2-5-by-colleen-hoover-some-of-our-fellow-readers-have-their-say/">http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/10/...</a><br /><br />We did want to share this thought. We recently asked Colleen Hoover why she wrote Finding Cinderella and why,instead of publishing it, did she decide to offer it to her readers for free and this was her response.<br /><br />COLLEEN:<br />Two reasons, really. The first is that it absolutely pains me to see comments from readers expressing that they’re looking forward to a book, but have to wait until payday. Or their birthday. Or Christmas. Eight dollars may not seem like much to some, but to others who are living on a budget, it’s hard to come by. I used to be one of those people who could only download the free books because eight dollars could buy my kids school lunches for a week. The second reason ties in to the first. My whole life has changed over the past two years and it’s hard not to feel a little undeserving for something so amazing. Sometimes I look around at all the great things that have happened and think, “What in the hell did I do to deserve this?” It’s hard to show gratitude through words when you’re as grateful as I am. I wanted my readers to know exactly how much they are appreciated and since it’s my stories they love, what better way to thank them than by giving them what they love for free. I just hope they like it!<br /><br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_734438638" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734438638" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734438638?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734438638" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9016636574361511014"><b>Finding Cinderella</b> made me fall in love with an insta-love romance! Seriously!<br/><br/>Daniel has a chance run-in with a girl in a maintenance closet, of all places. He’s had a mistake in his schedule and his 5th period slot was left empty. Daniel doesn’t point out the error, instead he uses the time for quality napping in the school maintenance closet. That’s until a girl stumbles in crying and his comforting leads to conversation and <i>more</i>. They only meet a couple of times, and keep their identities unk</span>
  <span id="freeText9016636574361511014" style="display:none"><b>Finding Cinderella</b> made me fall in love with an insta-love romance! Seriously!<br /><br />Daniel has a chance run-in with a girl in a maintenance closet, of all places. He’s had a mistake in his schedule and his 5th period slot was left empty. Daniel doesn’t point out the error, instead he uses the time for quality napping in the school maintenance closet. That’s until a girl stumbles in crying and his comforting leads to conversation and <i>more</i>. They only meet a couple of times, and keep their identities unknown, but their connection is intense and makes a lasting impression.<br /><br />Fast forward one year and Daniel meets Six. Six is like no other girl he’s known. He’s completely taken with her the minute he meets her, and Six seems to share the feeling. I’m not spoiling things by telling you that they are the couple from the closet, as it’s mentioned in the description, so as a reader you keep wondering when they’ll put it together. <br /><br />I never thought I’d be swayed by an insta-love romance, but I’m happy to be proved wrong. I was sucked in by the sweet, soaring highs both Daniel and Six experience from each other. They have such an intense effect on each other, and thankfully it’s mutual! They share all-consuming kisses, longing stares and can NOT keep their hands or lips off each other. While you think this is all a lighthearted swoony romance, there’s a heartbreaking surprise that sort of socks you in the gut. No worries, Colleen Hoover will leave a smile on your face in the end. <br /><br />This was only a 105 pages, and I know sometimes as a reader a novella can make you feel a little short changed in story at the end, but Ms. Hoover’s writing made every page count. She managed to make a small page count feel like such a large, wonderful story! <br /><br />Finding Cinderella is still free on Amazon, click <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Finding-Cinderella-A-Novella-ebook/dp/B00FNWRSCI/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1382596557&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=finding+cinderella" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE </a>for the link. <br /><br />You can find this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/10/review-finding-cinderella-by-colleen.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9016636574361511014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=high-school-romance">high-school-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730313860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5428860397481836572"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> "Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381777728ra/5291875.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i> "I feel <b>her</b> in every part of me and the feeling is new and heavy and intense and I realize in this moment that we just became so much more together than we could ever possibly be alone."</i>
</blockquote><br/>Oh my goodness, Colleen Hoover did it again. In a matter of a mere 93 pages, she made me laugh and cry and smile at the overwhelming amount of cuteness in this book. I adored every page of this and my only complaint is that I wis</span>
  <span id="freeText5428860397481836572" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> "Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381777728ra/5291875.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i> "I feel <b>her</b> in every part of me and the feeling is new and heavy and intense and I realize in this moment that we just became so much more together than we could ever possibly be alone."</i>
</blockquote><br>Oh my goodness, Colleen Hoover did it again. In a matter of a mere 93 pages, she made me laugh and cry and smile at the overwhelming amount of cuteness in this book. I adored every page of this and my only complaint is that I wish it were longer! I want more!!! Daniel and Six were freaking ADORABLE and I am glad to see Holder &amp; Sky's beloved besties get they're own not-so-fairy-tale happy every afters!<br><br>My Six &amp; Daniel:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381778413ra/5292335.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Is it cheating that I stole the actors from the movie "A Cinderella Story?" You gotta admit, they make the perfect Six and Daniel!)<br><br>Definitely one of my favourite novellas. I'll devour and love ANYTHING Ms.Hoover writes!</span>

  <b>
    <i>“It feels sort of euphoric, like we’re in some sort of fairytale. Like she’s Tinkerbell and I’m Peter Pan. <br/>No, wait. I don’t want to be Peter Pan. Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>That is an <b>insta-love</b> novella, but <b>I LOVED THIS!!</b> It's so funny and quick-read through exams. :)<br/>You can read it as a <b>stand-alone</b> or after reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1645010528?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Hopeless</a>. <br/><br/>It's about Six "Sky's friend" and Daniel "Holder's friend" and their love story.<br/>They are so funny and an amazing match! </span>
  <span id="freeText4653192740593896328" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It feels sort of euphoric, like we’re in some sort of fairytale. Like she’s Tinkerbell and I’m Peter Pan. <br>No, wait. I don’t want to be Peter Pan. Maybe she can be like Cinderella and I’ll be her Prince Charming”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>That is an <b>insta-love</b> novella, but <b>I LOVED THIS!!</b> It's so funny and quick-read through exams. :)<br>You can read it as a <b>stand-alone</b> or after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1645010528?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Hopeless</a>. <br><br>It's about Six "Sky's friend" and Daniel "Holder's friend" and their love story.<br>They are so funny and an amazing match! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464735305i/19270233._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_732440315" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/732440315" />
    <a title="Liis McKinstry" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16807207-liis-mckinstry"><img alt="Liis McKinstry" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394981529p2/16807207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/732440315?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liis McKinstry" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liis McKinstry" href="/user/show/16807207-liis-mckinstry">Liis McKinstry</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer732440315" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9503412143304894135">>>>>><br/><br/>I’ve NEVER been so angry at those little signs in my life. They’ve always behaved; minded their own business; stayed out of my books.<br/><br/>Until Colleen BUTTERFLYING Hoover put them in the copy of Finding Cinderella that was sent to me. And now all I want to do is kick the a** of the person that came up with them.<br/><br/>Now I know the novella is not out yet, you’re probably very jealous, but I got it through legitimate means, so suck it! You have two things going for you though; one – it will be out to </span>
  <span id="freeText9503412143304894135" style="display:none">&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;<br /><br />I’ve NEVER been so angry at those little signs in my life. They’ve always behaved; minded their own business; stayed out of my books.<br /><br />Until Colleen BUTTERFLYING Hoover put them in the copy of Finding Cinderella that was sent to me. And now all I want to do is kick the a** of the person that came up with them.<br /><br />Now I know the novella is not out yet, you’re probably very jealous, but I got it through legitimate means, so suck it! You have two things going for you though; one – it will be out to the masses in November, and two – it’ll be FREE!<br /><br />If you’re a fan of Colleen Hoover, you’ll know who Daniel and Six are. If you are a fan of Colleen Hoover and think I’m talking about Daniel Craig and the number 6, you’re nuts and shouldn’t read the rest of this...I SAID STOP!<br /><br />Okay, so this a novella told from Daniel’s POV.<br /><br />................................................................it’s really hard to compliment an author when your words might be misconstrued as insults to their previous works. So let’s clear the air. I adored Slammed. Fiended for Point of Retreat. Fell hopelessly in love with Hopeless. Wanted to make Losing Hope into a pillow so I could hug it every night while I slept with it.<br /><br />While reading Finding Cinderella, I was like, Holder who? Will? Don’t know a Will. Now Daniel...yeah! This novella is THAT good. Screw good, it’s THAT eating-Reese’s-Pieces-on-top-on-french-vanilla-ice-cream-while-watching-a-YouTube-video-of-IandLOVEandYOU amazing!<br /><br />The characters that I loved in Hopeless and Losing Hope make appearances, but to be honest, I never for a moment thought of them or their stories. This is the story of Daniel and Six, and Ms. Hoover never deviates for that.<br /><br />It’s been a while since I’ve laughed so honestly while reading a book. I don’t think there’s anyone out there who can take ‘It’s a human?’ and have the reader almost pee their pants, and then subsequently get the hiccups from laughing for 5 (not six – god I’m funny!) minutes straight.<br /><br />I’ve also had by heart shattered by books countless times. And this story took an over-sized sledgehammer to my ever-fragile organ. I can’t really talk about the story too much without giving stuff away. So when you get the notice that Finding Cinderella is LIVE, go and download it immediately. Then drink a large coffee with an espresso-shot so you can read it right away.<br /> <br />The only fault I found with this story was that it ended. And those &gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;! GAH!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9503412143304894135" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_733044517" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733044517" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/733044517?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18593175-finding-cinderella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733044517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6889159499957914316"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381981358i/5504142._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Although Finding Cinderella can be read as a standalone, everyone should read Hopeless and Losing Hope. Not because it’s required to fully understand this novella, but because Colleen Hoover created an exceptional story and everyone should experience it.</i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381775ra/739207.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For those of us who have already read Losing Hope, we know about Daniel’s maintenance room experience. We all knew instantly that his girl was Six. But now we get to see it unfold. We get a chance to experience that day when their world changed, </span>
  <span id="freeText6889159499957914316" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381981358i/5504142._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Although Finding Cinderella can be read as a standalone, everyone should read Hopeless and Losing Hope. Not because it’s required to fully understand this novella, but because Colleen Hoover created an exceptional story and everyone should experience it.</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381775ra/739207.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For those of us who have already read Losing Hope, we know about Daniel’s maintenance room experience. We all knew instantly that his girl was Six. But now we get to see it unfold. We get a chance to experience that day when their world changed, even if they didn't realize it until a year later.<br>I seriously tried hard to pull specific quotes out of this for the sole purpose of this review, and looking back now at them I realized that entire sections and pages are adorned in yellow. Every single word of this story was loved. <br><br>I had not known what to expect from Daniel since we only really got to know him through Holder’s eyes. He was sarcastic and a bit immature, but he was loyal. And holy smokes did he completely make me swoon. <br><br>Although Daniel and Six easily fit at the start of this story as two strangers who are free to discuss their fears in the cloak of darkness, but where this story gave me butterflies was as Daniel falls for Six a year later before he realizes that she was that girl.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381981358ra/5504144.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>His moments with Six were down right perfection. CoHo creates the perfect book boyfriends every damn time. The way he was able to go from fun to tender had my knees weak and seriously fighting stabs of jealousy over a fictional character. <br><br><i>Is it wrong that I thought ‘Michelle” every time he said Six? </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401940ra/780721.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I absolutely loved this novella and I love that Colleen was so gracious to give us all a little more of these four characters that completely own a piece of my heart. The Hopeless Series is one of those stories that I will never forget.</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6889159499957914316" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aN5F5uSo9icf1uGR5iLkKeFVlLKYNmu6CL9O0okAf7NS+Cw0X/Y/T7j9VfAR1+72Nwpzela75d1TwQhjREONKQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3wE59Yzlig5dPPGnIKkkPrUlqQcsYNL7xpD3RhnEKMflJ1AnN7tDZvoXRcbXXC7hY3pOz+LtXJyd7rH31IfaXQ==')})
  }

Colleen Hoover exercises her creativity, to depict a contemporary love story, Maybe Someday. The narrative is driven by themes of love, music, love of music and thoroughly modern form of communication. Shakespeare wrote in Twelfth Night, “If music be the food of love, play on!” Music is most decidedly the food of love in this novel, and they do indeed play on -- right up until the end.  Maybe Someday was written with a definite target audience in mind. This book will appeal to older teens and young adults, particularly females. For others, it will appear somewhat similar to other love stories that they will have read in the past that deals with love triangles, and the pain, joy and complications that surround relationships. What sets it apart, however, is the unique approach that Colleen Hoover takes.  She has created a novel that incorporates music as an essential theme while, at the same time, her main male protagonist is deaf. It imbues the story with an interesting angle. The innovative touches in Maybe Someday saves the novel from being formulaic, and it is filled with wonderful emotional expressiveness.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"1500552458794337346\" href=\"#\"
